030/**
031 * Test various scientific and non scientific names to parse.
032 * TODO: Add tests for the following names found unparsed in CLB:
033 * (?) Physignathus cochinchinensis Guérin, 1829
034 * (Acmaeops)
035 * (Acmaeops) rufula Gardiner, 1970
036 * (Amsel, 1935)
037 * (Antopocerus)
038 * (Arocephalus) languidus (Flor, 1861)
039 * (Athysanella) salsa (Ball & Beamer, 1940)
040 * (Erdianus) nigricans (Kirschbaum, 1868)
041 * ? Callidium
042 * ? Callidium (Phymatodes)
043 * ? Callidium (Phymatodes) semicircularis Bland, 1862
044 * ? Compsa
045 * ? Compsa flavofasciata Martins & Galileo, 2002
046 */
047public class NameParserTest {
048
049  private static Logger LOG = LoggerFactory.getLogger(NameParserTest.class);
050  private static final InputStreamUtils streamUtils = new InputStreamUtils();
051  private NameParser parser = new NameParser(50);
052
053  private void assertHybridFormula(String name) {
054    try {
055      parser.parse(name, null);
056    } catch (UnparsableException e) {
057      assertEquals(NameType.HYBRID, e.type);
058    }
059  }
060
061  private void assertHybridName(ParsedName pn) {
062    assertTrue(NameType.HYBRID != pn.getType());
063    assertTrue(pn.canonicalNameWithMarker().length() > 8);
064  }
065
066  private void assertUnparsableType(NameType type, String name) {
067    try {
068      parser.parse(name, null);
069      fail("Name should be an unparsable " + type + ": " + name);
070    } catch (UnparsableException e) {
071      assertEquals(type, e.type);
072    }
073  }
074
075  private void assertNoName(String name) {
076    assertUnparsableType(NameType.NO_NAME, name);
077  }
078
079  private void assertUnparsableDoubtful(String name) {
080    try {
081      parser.parse(name, null);
082      fail("Name should be unparsable: " + name);
083    } catch (UnparsableException e) {
084      assertEquals(NameType.DOUBTFUL, e.type);
085    }
086  }
087
088  private void allowUnparsable(String name) {
089    try {
090      parser.parse(name, null);
091    } catch (UnparsableException e) {
092    }
093  }
094
095  // 0scientificName
096  // 1genusOrAbove
097  // 2infraGeneric
098  // 3specificEpithet
099  // 4infraSpecificEpithet
100  // 5 cultivarEpithet
101  // 6authorship
102  // 7year
103  // 8bracketAuthorship
104  // 9bracketYear
105  // 10rank
106  // 11nomcode
107  // 12nothotype
108  // 13nametype
109  private ParsedName buildParsedNameFromTabRow(String[] cols) {
110    try {
111      return new ParsedName(NameType.fromString(cols[13]), StringUtils.trimToNull(cols[1]),
112          StringUtils.trimToNull(cols[2]), StringUtils.trimToNull(cols[3]), StringUtils.trimToNull(cols[4]),
113          NamePart.fromString(cols[12]), RankUtils.inferRank(StringUtils.trimToNull(cols[10])), StringUtils.trimToNull(cols[6]),
114          StringUtils.trimToNull(cols[7]), StringUtils.trimToNull(cols[8]), StringUtils.trimToNull(cols[9]),
115          StringUtils.trimToNull(cols[5]), null, null, null, null);
116
117    } catch (ArrayIndexOutOfBoundsException e) {
118      LOG.error("scientific_names.txt file bogus, too little columns:\n{}", Joiner.on("|").useForNull("").join(cols));
119      throw e;
120    }
121  }
122
123  private String extractNomNote(String name) {
124    String nomNote = null;
125    Matcher matcher = NameParser.EXTRACT_NOMSTATUS.matcher(name);
126    if (matcher.find()) {
127      nomNote = (StringUtils.trimToNull(matcher.group(1)));
128    }
129    return nomNote;
130  }
131
132  @Test
133  public void test4PartedNames() throws Exception {
134    ParsedName n = parser.parse("Bombus sichelii alticola latofasciatus", null);
135    assertEquals("Bombus sichelii latofasciatus", n.canonicalName());
136    assertEquals("Bombus sichelii infrasubsp. latofasciatus", n.canonicalNameWithMarker());
137
138    n = parser.parse("Bombus sichelii alticola latofasciatus Vogt, 1909", null);
139    assertEquals("Bombus sichelii latofasciatus", n.canonicalName());
140    assertEquals("Bombus sichelii infrasubsp. latofasciatus", n.canonicalNameWithMarker());
141    assertEquals("Bombus sichelii infrasubsp. latofasciatus Vogt, 1909", n.canonicalNameComplete());
142
143    n = parser.parse("Poa pratensis kewensis proles (L.) Rouy, 1913", null);
144    assertEquals("Poa", n.getGenusOrAbove());
145    assertEquals("pratensis", n.getSpecificEpithet());
146    assertEquals("proles", n.getInfraSpecificEpithet());
147    assertEquals("Rouy", n.getAuthorship());
148    assertEquals("1913", n.getYear());
149    assertEquals("L.", n.getBracketAuthorship());
150    assertNull(n.getBracketYear());
151    assertEquals(NameType.SCIENTIFIC, n.getType());
152    assertEquals("Poa pratensis proles", n.canonicalName());
153    assertEquals("Poa pratensis infrasubsp. proles", n.canonicalNameWithMarker());
154    assertEquals("Poa pratensis infrasubsp. proles (L.) Rouy, 1913", n.canonicalNameComplete());
155  }
156
157  private boolean testAuthorship(String author) {
158    Matcher m = NormalisedNameParser.AUTHOR_TEAM_PATTERN.matcher(author);
159    if (m.find()) {
160      return true;
161    } else {
162      return false;
163    }
164  }
165
166  /**
167   * Avoid NPEs and other exceptions for very short non names and other extremes found in occurrences.
168   */
169  @Test
170  public void testAvoidNPE() throws Exception {
171    allowUnparsable(null);
172    allowUnparsable(" ");
173    allowUnparsable("");
174    allowUnparsable("\"");
175    allowUnparsable("\\");
176    allowUnparsable(".");
177    allowUnparsable("a");
178    allowUnparsable("'");
179    allowUnparsable("von");
180    allowUnparsable("X");
181    allowUnparsable("@");
182    allowUnparsable("&nbsp;");
183    allowUnparsable("\"? gryphoidis");
184  }

232  @Test
233  public void testNotNames() throws Exception {
234    ParsedName pn = parser.parse("Diatrypella favacea var. favacea (Fr.) Ces. & De Not.", null);
235    assertEquals("Diatrypella", pn.getGenusOrAbove());
236    assertEquals("favacea", pn.getSpecificEpithet());
237    assertEquals(Rank.VARIETY, pn.getRank());
238    assertEquals("favacea", pn.getInfraSpecificEpithet());
239    assertEquals("Ces. & De Not.", pn.getAuthorship());
240    assertEquals("Fr.", pn.getBracketAuthorship());
241
242    pn = parser.parse("Protoventuria rosae (De Not.) Berl. & Sacc.", null);
243    assertEquals("Protoventuria", pn.getGenusOrAbove());
244    assertEquals("rosae", pn.getSpecificEpithet());
245    assertEquals("Berl. & Sacc.", pn.getAuthorship());
246    assertEquals("De Not.", pn.getBracketAuthorship());
247
248    pn = parser.parse("Hormospora De Not.", null);
249    assertEquals("Hormospora", pn.getGenusOrAbove());
250    assertEquals("De Not.", pn.getAuthorship());
251  }

253  @Test
254  public void testCanonNameParserSubgenera() throws Exception {
255    ParsedName pn = parser.parse("Polygonum subgen. Bistorta (L.) Zernov", null);
256    assertNull(pn.getNotho());
257    assertEquals("Polygonum", pn.getGenusOrAbove());
258    assertEquals("Bistorta", pn.getInfraGeneric());
259    assertEquals(Rank.SUBGENUS, pn.getRank());
260    assertEquals("Zernov", pn.getAuthorship());
261    assertEquals("L.", pn.getBracketAuthorship());
262
263    ParsedName n = parser.parse("Arrhoges (Antarctohoges)", null);
264    assertEquals("Arrhoges", n.getGenusOrAbove());
265    assertEquals("Antarctohoges", n.getBracketAuthorship());
266    assertNull(n.getInfraGeneric());
267    assertNull(n.getRank());
268    assertNull(n.getNotho());
269
270    n = parser.parse("Arrhoges (Antarctohoges)", Rank.SUBGENUS);
271    assertEquals("Arrhoges", n.getGenusOrAbove());
272    assertEquals("Antarctohoges", n.getInfraGeneric());
273    assertEquals(Rank.SUBGENUS, n.getRank());
274    assertNull(n.getNotho());
275
276    pn = parser.parse("Festuca subg. Schedonorus (P. Beauv. ) Peterm.", null);
277    assertEquals("Festuca", pn.getGenusOrAbove());
278    assertEquals("Schedonorus", pn.getInfraGeneric());
279    assertEquals(Rank.SUBGENUS, pn.getRank());
280    assertEquals("Peterm.", pn.getAuthorship());
281    assertEquals("P. Beauv.", pn.getBracketAuthorship());
282
283    n = parser.parse("Catapodium subg.Agropyropsis  Trab.", null);
284    assertEquals("Catapodium", n.getGenusOrAbove());
285    assertEquals("Agropyropsis", n.getInfraGeneric());
286    assertEquals(Rank.SUBGENUS, n.getRank());
287
288    n = parser.parse(" Gnaphalium subg. Laphangium Hilliard & B. L. Burtt", null);
289    assertEquals("Gnaphalium", n.getGenusOrAbove());
290    assertEquals("Laphangium", n.getInfraGeneric());
291    assertEquals(Rank.SUBGENUS, n.getRank());
292
293    n = parser.parse("Woodsiaceae (Hooker) Herter", null);
294    assertEquals("Woodsiaceae", n.getGenusOrAbove());
295    assertNull(n.getInfraGeneric());
296    assertEquals(Rank.FAMILY, n.getRank());
297  }

299  @Test
300  public void testClean1() throws Exception {
301    assertEquals("", NameParser.preClean(""));
302    assertEquals("Hallo Spencer", NameParser.preClean("Hallo Spencer "));
303    assertEquals("Hallo Spencer", NameParser.preClean("' 'Hallo Spencer"));
304    assertEquals("Hallo Spencer 1982", NameParser.preClean("'\" Hallo  Spencer 1982'"));
305  }
306
307  private boolean testCultivar(String cultivar) {
308    Matcher m = NameParser.CULTIVAR.matcher(cultivar);
309    if (m.find()) {
310      return true;
311    } else {
312      return false;
313    }
314  }
315
316  private ParsedName parseCandidatus(String name, String expectedGenus, String expectedSpecies, String expectedInfraSpecies)
317      throws UnparsableException {
318    ParsedName pn = parser.parse(name, null);
319    assertEquals(NameType.CANDIDATUS, pn.getType());
320
321    assertEquals(Strings.nullToEmpty(expectedGenus), Strings.nullToEmpty(pn.getGenusOrAbove()));
322    assertEquals(Strings.nullToEmpty(expectedSpecies), Strings.nullToEmpty(pn.getSpecificEpithet()));
323    assertEquals(Strings.nullToEmpty(expectedInfraSpecies), Strings.nullToEmpty(pn.getInfraSpecificEpithet()));
324
325    return pn;
326  }
327
328  @Test
329  public void testCandidatus() throws Exception {
330    ParsedName pn = parseCandidatus("\"Candidatus Endowatersipora\" Anderson and Haygood, 2007", "Endowatersipora", null, null);
331    assertEquals("Anderson & Haygood", pn.getAuthorship());
332    assertEquals("2007", pn.getYear());
333
334    pn = parseCandidatus("Candidatus Phytoplasma allocasuarinae", "Phytoplasma", "allocasuarinae", null);
335
336    pn = parseCandidatus("Ca. Phytoplasma allocasuarinae", "Phytoplasma", "allocasuarinae", null);
337
338    pn = parseCandidatus("Candidatus Phytoplasma", "Phytoplasma", null, null);
339    pn = parseCandidatus("Ca. Phytoplasma", "Phytoplasma", null, null);
340
341    pn = parseCandidatus("'Candidatus Nicolleia'", "Nicolleia", null, null);
342
343
344    pn = parseCandidatus("\"Candidatus Riegeria\" Gruber-Vodicka et al., 2011", "Riegeria", null, null);
345    assertEquals("Gruber-Vodicka et al.", pn.getAuthorship());
346    assertEquals("2011", pn.getYear());
347
348    //TODO: parse strains
349    //pn = parseCandidatus("Candidatus Midichloria sp. ixholo1", "Midichloria", "ixholo1",null);
350    //pn = parseCandidatus("Candidatus Endobugula sp. JYr4", "Endobugula", "JYr4",null);
351
352  }

357  @Test
358  public void testExNames() throws Exception {
359    ParsedName pn = assertExAuthorName(parser.parse("Abies brevifolia cv. ex Dallim.", null));
360    pn = assertExAuthorName(parser.parse("Abies brevifolia hort. ex Dallim.", null));
361    pn = assertExAuthorName(parser.parse("Abutilon bastardioides Baker f. ex Rose", null));
362    pn = assertExAuthorName(parser.parse("Acacia truncata (Burm. f.) hort. ex Hoffmanns.", null));
363    pn = assertExAuthorName(parser.parse("Anoectocalyx ex Cogn. 'Triana'", null));
364    pn = assertExAuthorName(parser.parse("Anoectocalyx \"Triana\" ex Cogn.  ", null));
365    pn = assertExAuthorName(parser.parse("Aukuba ex Koehne 'Thunb'   ", null));
366    pn = assertExAuthorName(parser.parse("Crepinella subgen. Marchal ex Oliver  ", null));
367    pn = assertExAuthorName(parser.parse("Echinocereus sect. Triglochidiata ex Bravo", null));
368    pn = assertExAuthorName(parser.parse("Hadrolaelia sect. Sophronitis ex Chiron & V.P.Castro", null));
369
370    pn = assertExAuthorName(parser.parse("Abutilon ×hybridum cv. ex Voss", null));
371  }
372
373  private ParsedName assertExAuthorName(ParsedName pn) {
374    assertFalse("ex".equalsIgnoreCase(pn.getSpecificEpithet()));
375    assertFalse("ex".equalsIgnoreCase(pn.getInfraSpecificEpithet()));
376    assertFalse("ex".equalsIgnoreCase(pn.getInfraGeneric()));
377    assertNotNull(pn.getGenusOrAbove());
378    return pn;
379  }

381  @Test
382  //@Ignore("needs a parser update, just added for test first approach")
383  public void testCultivarNames() throws Exception {
384    ParsedName pn = parser.parse("Verpericola megasoma \"Dall\" Pils.", null);
385
386
387    pn = parser.parse("Abutilon 'Kentish Belle'", null);
388    assertEquals("Abutilon", pn.getGenusOrAbove());
389    assertEquals("Kentish Belle", pn.getCultivarEpithet());
390    assertEquals(NameType.CULTIVAR, pn.getType());
391
392    pn = parser.parse("Abutilon 'Nabob'", null);
393    assertEquals("Abutilon", pn.getGenusOrAbove());
394    assertEquals("Nabob", pn.getCultivarEpithet());
395    assertEquals(NameType.CULTIVAR, pn.getType());
396
397    pn = parser.parse("Verpericola megasoma \"Dall\" Pils.", null);
398    assertEquals("Verpericola", pn.getGenusOrAbove());
399    assertEquals("megasoma", pn.getSpecificEpithet());
400    assertEquals("Dall", pn.getCultivarEpithet());
401    assertEquals("Pils.", pn.getAuthorship());
402    assertEquals(NameType.CULTIVAR, pn.getType());
403
404    pn = parser.parse("Sorbus americana Marshall cv. 'Belmonte'", null);
405    assertEquals("Sorbus", pn.getGenusOrAbove());
406    assertEquals("americana", pn.getSpecificEpithet());
407    assertEquals("Belmonte", pn.getCultivarEpithet());
408    assertEquals(NameType.CULTIVAR, pn.getType());
409
410    pn = parser.parse("Sorbus hupehensis C.K.Schneid. cv. 'November pink'", null);
411    assertEquals("Sorbus", pn.getGenusOrAbove());
412    assertEquals("hupehensis", pn.getSpecificEpithet());
413    assertEquals("November pink", pn.getCultivarEpithet());
414    assertEquals(NameType.CULTIVAR, pn.getType());
415
416    pn = parser.parse("Symphoricarpos albus (L.) S.F.Blake cv. 'Turesson'", null);
417    assertEquals("Symphoricarpos", pn.getGenusOrAbove());
418    assertEquals("albus", pn.getSpecificEpithet());
419    assertEquals("Turesson", pn.getCultivarEpithet());
420    assertEquals(NameType.CULTIVAR, pn.getType());
421    assertEquals(Rank.CULTIVAR, pn.getRank());
422
423    pn = parser.parse("Symphoricarpos sp. cv. 'mother of pearl'", null);
424    assertEquals("Symphoricarpos", pn.getGenusOrAbove());
425    assertEquals("mother of pearl", pn.getCultivarEpithet());
426    assertEquals(NameType.CULTIVAR, pn.getType());
427    assertEquals(Rank.CULTIVAR, pn.getRank());
428
429    pn = parser.parse("Primula Border Auricula Group", null);
430    assertEquals("Primula", pn.getGenusOrAbove());
431    assertEquals("Border Auricula", pn.getCultivarEpithet());
432    assertEquals(NameType.CULTIVAR, pn.getType());
433    assertEquals(Rank.CULTIVAR_GROUP, pn.getRank());
434
435    pn = parser.parse("Rhododendron boothii Mishmiense Group", null);
436    assertEquals("Rhododendron", pn.getGenusOrAbove());
437    assertEquals("boothii", pn.getSpecificEpithet());
438    assertEquals("Mishmiense", pn.getCultivarEpithet());
439    assertEquals(NameType.CULTIVAR, pn.getType());
440    assertEquals(Rank.CULTIVAR_GROUP, pn.getRank());
441
442    pn = parser.parse("Paphiopedilum Sorel grex", null);
443    assertEquals("Paphiopedilum", pn.getGenusOrAbove());
444    assertNull(pn.getSpecificEpithet());
445    assertEquals("Sorel", pn.getCultivarEpithet());
446    assertEquals(NameType.CULTIVAR, pn.getType());
447    assertEquals(Rank.GREX, pn.getRank());
448  }

450  @Test
451  public void testCultivarPattern() throws Exception {
452    assertTrue(this.testCultivar("'Kentish Belle'"));
453    assertTrue(this.testCultivar("'Nabob'"));
454    assertTrue(this.testCultivar("\"Dall\""));
455    assertTrue(this.testCultivar(" cv. 'Belmonte'"));
456    assertTrue(this.testCultivar("Sorbus hupehensis C.K.Schneid. cv. 'November pink'"));
457    assertTrue(this.testCultivar("Symphoricarpos albus (L.) S.F.Blake cv. 'Turesson'"));
458    assertTrue(this.testCultivar("Symphoricarpos sp. cv. 'mother of pearl'"));
459
460  }

462  @Test
463  public void testEscaping() throws Exception {
464    assertEquals("Caloplaca poliotera (Nyl.) J. Steiner",
465        parser.normalize("Caloplaca poliotera (Nyl.) J. Steiner\\r\\n\\r\\n"));
466
467    ParsedName pn = parser.parse("Caloplaca poliotera (Nyl.) J. Steiner\\r\\n\\r\\n.", null);
468    assertNull(pn.getNotho());
469    assertEquals("Caloplaca", pn.getGenusOrAbove());
470    assertEquals("poliotera", pn.getSpecificEpithet());
471    assertEquals("Nyl.", pn.getBracketAuthorship());
472    assertEquals("J. Steiner", pn.getAuthorship());
473  }

475  @Test
476  public void testHybridFormulas() throws Exception {
477    assertHybridFormula("Arthopyrenia hyalospora X Hydnellum scrobiculatum");
478    assertHybridFormula("Arthopyrenia hyalospora (Banker) D. Hall X Hydnellum scrobiculatum D.E. Stuntz");
479    assertHybridFormula("Arthopyrenia hyalospora × ? ");
480    assertHybridFormula("Agrostis L. × Polypogon Desf. ");
481    assertHybridFormula("Agrostis stolonifera L. × Polypogon monspeliensis (L.) Desf. ");
482    assertHybridFormula("Asplenium rhizophyllum X A. ruta-muraria E.L. Braun 1939");
483    assertHybridFormula("Asplenium rhizophyllum DC. x ruta-muraria E.L. Braun 1939");
484    assertHybridFormula("Asplenium rhizophyllum x ruta-muraria");
485    assertHybridFormula("Salix aurita L. × S. caprea L.");
486    assertHybridFormula("Mentha aquatica L. × M. arvensis L. × M. spicata L.");
487    assertHybridFormula("Polypodium vulgare subsp. prionodes (Asch.) Rothm. × subsp. vulgare");
488    assertHybridFormula("Tilletia caries (Bjerk.) Tul. × T. foetida (Wallr.) Liro.");
489
490    assertEquals("Polypodium vulgare nothosubsp. mantoniae (Rothm.) Schidlay", parser.parse("Polypodium  x vulgare nothosubsp. mantoniae (Rothm.) Schidlay ", null).fullName());
491    assertHybridName(parser.parse("Arthopyrenia hyalospora x ", null));
492  }

494  @Test
495  public void testHybridAlikeNames() throws Exception {
496    ParsedName n = parser.parse("Huaiyuanella Xing, Yan & Yin, 1984", null);
497    assertNull(n.getNotho());
498    assertEquals("Huaiyuanella", n.getGenusOrAbove());
499    assertNull(n.getSpecificEpithet());
500    assertEquals("Xing, Yan & Yin", n.getAuthorship());
501    assertEquals("1984", n.getYear());
502
503    n = parser.parse("Caveasphaera Xiao & Knoll, 2000", null);
504    assertNull(n.getNotho());
505    assertEquals("Caveasphaera", n.getGenusOrAbove());
506    assertNull(n.getSpecificEpithet());
507    assertEquals("2000", n.getYear());

696  @Test
697  public void testVirusNames() throws Exception {
698    ParsedName pn = parser.parse("Crassatellites janus Hedley, 1906", null);
699    assertEquals("Crassatellites", pn.getGenusOrAbove());
700    assertEquals("janus", pn.getSpecificEpithet());
701    assertEquals("Hedley", pn.getAuthorship());
702    assertEquals("1906", pn.getYear());
703
704    pn = parser.parse("Ypsolophus satellitella", null);
705    assertEquals("Ypsolophus", pn.getGenusOrAbove());
706    assertEquals("satellitella", pn.getSpecificEpithet());
707
708    pn = parser.parse("Nephodia satellites", null);
709    assertEquals("Nephodia", pn.getGenusOrAbove());
710    assertEquals("satellites", pn.getSpecificEpithet());
711
712    Reader reader = FileUtils.getInputStreamReader(streamUtils.classpathStream("viruses.txt"));
713    LineIterator iter = new LineIterator(reader);
714    while (iter.hasNext()) {
715      String line = iter.nextLine();
716      if (line == null || line.startsWith("#") || line.trim().isEmpty()) {
717        continue;
718      }
719      assertUnparsableType(NameType.VIRUS, line);
720    }
721  }

739  @Test
740  public void testEbiUncultured() throws Exception {
741    assertUnparsableType(NameType.PLACEHOLDER, "uncultured Verrucomicrobiales bacterium");
742    assertUnparsableType(NameType.PLACEHOLDER, "uncultured Verrucomicrobium sp.");
743    assertUnparsableType(NameType.PLACEHOLDER, "uncultured Verrucomicrobia bacterium");
744    assertUnparsableType(NameType.PLACEHOLDER, "uncultured Vibrio sp.");
745    assertUnparsableType(NameType.PLACEHOLDER, "uncultured Wilcoxina");
746    assertUnparsableType(NameType.PLACEHOLDER, "uncultured zygomycete");
747    assertUnparsableType(NameType.PLACEHOLDER, "uncultured Yonghaparkia sp");
748    assertUnparsableType(NameType.PLACEHOLDER, "uncultured virus");
749    // other placeholders e.g from ITIS:
750    assertUnparsableType(NameType.PLACEHOLDER, "Temp dummy name");
751  }

767    assertEquals("Candida", pn.getGenusOrAbove());

783    assertEquals(NameType.INFORMAL, pn.getType());

790  @Test
791  public void testIndetParsering() throws Exception {
792    ParsedName pn = parser.parse("Polygonum spec.", null);
793    assertEquals("Polygonum", pn.getGenusOrAbove());
794    assertNull(pn.getSpecificEpithet());
795    assertEquals(Rank.SPECIES, pn.getRank());
796    assertEquals(NameType.INFORMAL, pn.getType());
797
798    pn = parser.parse("Polygonum vulgaris ssp.", null);
799    assertEquals("Polygonum", pn.getGenusOrAbove());
800    assertEquals("vulgaris", pn.getSpecificEpithet());
801    assertEquals(Rank.SUBSPECIES, pn.getRank());
802    assertEquals(NameType.INFORMAL, pn.getType());
803
804    pn = parser.parse("Mesocricetus sp.", null);
805    assertEquals("Mesocricetus", pn.getGenusOrAbove());
806    assertNull(pn.getSpecificEpithet());
807    assertEquals(Rank.SPECIES, pn.getRank());
808    assertEquals(NameType.INFORMAL, pn.getType());
809
810    // also treat these bacterial names as indets
811    pn = parser.parse("Bartonella sp. RN, 10623LA", null);
812    assertEquals("Bartonella", pn.getGenusOrAbove());
813    assertEquals(Rank.SPECIES, pn.getRank());
814    assertEquals(NameType.INFORMAL, pn.getType());
815
816    // and dont treat these authorships as forms
817    pn = parser.parse("Dioscoreales Hooker f.", null);
818    assertEquals("Dioscoreales", pn.getGenusOrAbove());
819    assertEquals("Hooker f.", pn.getAuthorship());
820    assertEquals(Rank.ORDER, pn.getRank());
821    assertEquals(NameType.SCIENTIFIC, pn.getType());
822
823    pn = parser.parse("Lepidoptera sp. JGP0404", null);
824    assertEquals("Lepidoptera", pn.getGenusOrAbove());
825    assertNull(pn.getSpecificEpithet());
826    assertNull(pn.getAuthorship());
827    assertEquals(Rank.SPECIES, pn.getRank());
828    assertEquals(NameType.INFORMAL, pn.getType());
829
830    pn = parser.parse("Melastoma vacillans Blume var.", null);
831
832    pn = parser.parse("Lepidoptera Hooker", Rank.SPECIES);
833    assertEquals("Lepidoptera", pn.getGenusOrAbove());
834    assertNull(pn.getSpecificEpithet());
835    assertEquals("Hooker", pn.getAuthorship());
836    assertEquals(Rank.SPECIES, pn.getRank());
837    assertEquals(NameType.INFORMAL, pn.getType());
838
839    pn = parser.parse("Lepidoptera alba DC.", Rank.SUBSPECIES);
840    assertEquals("Lepidoptera", pn.getGenusOrAbove());
841    assertEquals("alba", pn.getSpecificEpithet());
842    assertEquals("DC.", pn.getAuthorship());
843    assertEquals(Rank.SUBSPECIES, pn.getRank());
844    assertEquals(NameType.INFORMAL, pn.getType());
845
846    pn = parser.parse("Lepidoptera alba DC.", Rank.SUBSPECIES);
847    assertEquals("Lepidoptera", pn.getGenusOrAbove());
848    assertEquals("alba", pn.getSpecificEpithet());
849    assertEquals("DC.", pn.getAuthorship());
850    assertEquals(Rank.SUBSPECIES, pn.getRank());
851    assertEquals(NameType.INFORMAL, pn.getType());
852  }

854  @Test

858    assertNull(pn.getSpecificEpithet());
859    assertEquals(Rank.SUBGENUS, pn.getRank());
860    assertEquals(NameType.SCIENTIFIC, pn.getType());
861
862    pn = parser.parse("Polygonum", Rank.SUBSPECIES);
863    assertEquals("Polygonum", pn.getGenusOrAbove());
864    assertNull(pn.getSpecificEpithet());
865    assertNull(pn.getAuthorship());
866    assertEquals(Rank.SUBSPECIES, pn.getRank());
867    assertEquals(NameType.INFORMAL, pn.getType());
868
869    pn = parser.parse("Polygonum alba", Rank.GENUS);
870    assertEquals("Polygonum", pn.getGenusOrAbove());
871    assertEquals("alba", pn.getSpecificEpithet());
872    assertNull(pn.getAuthorship());
873    assertEquals(Rank.GENUS, pn.getRank());
874    assertEquals(NameType.DOUBTFUL, pn.getType());
875
876    pn = parser.parse("Polygonum", Rank.CULTIVAR);
877    assertEquals("Polygonum", pn.getGenusOrAbove());
878    assertNull(pn.getSpecificEpithet());
879    assertNull(pn.getAuthorship());

881    assertEquals(NameType.INFORMAL, pn.getType());

884  @Test
885  public void testTimeoutNameFile() throws Exception {
886    Reader reader = FileUtils.getInputStreamReader(streamUtils.classpathStream("timeout-names.txt"));
887    LineIterator iter = new LineIterator(reader);
888    while (iter.hasNext()) {
889      String line = iter.nextLine();
890      if (line == null || line.startsWith("#") || line.trim().isEmpty()) {
891        continue;
892      }
893      ParsedName n = parser.parse(line, null);
894    }
895  }

4773
4774  @Test
4775  public void testNameParserCanonical() throws Exception {
4776
4777    assertEquals("Abelia grandifolia", parser.parseToCanonical("Abelia grandifolia Villarreal, 2000 Villarreal, 2000", null));
4778    assertEquals("Abelia macrotera",
4779        parser.parseToCanonical("Abelia macrotera (Graebn. & Buchw.) Rehder (Graebn. et Buchw.) Rehder", null));
4780    assertEquals("Abelia mexicana", parser.parseToCanonical("Abelia mexicana Villarreal, 2000 Villarreal, 2000", null));
4781    assertEquals("Abelia serrata", parser.parseToCanonical("Abelia serrata Abelia serrata Siebold & Zucc.", null));
4782    assertEquals("Abelia spathulata colorata", parser.parseToCanonical(
4783        "Abelia spathulata colorata (Hara & Kurosawa) Hara & Kurosawa (Hara et Kurosawa) Hara et Kurosawa", null));
4784    assertEquals("Abelia tetrasepala",
4785        parser.parseToCanonical("Abelia tetrasepala (Koidz.) H.Hara & S.Kuros. (Koidz.) H.Hara et S.Kuros.", null));
4786    assertEquals("Abelia tetrasepala",
4787        parser.parseToCanonical("Abelia tetrasepala (Koidz.) Hara & Kurosawa (Koidz.) Hara et Kurosawa", null));
4788    assertEquals("Abelmoschus esculentus",
4789        parser.parseToCanonical("Abelmoschus esculentus Abelmoschus esculentus (L.) Moench", null));
4790    assertEquals("Abelmoschus moschatus",
4791        parser.parseToCanonical("Abelmoschus moschatus Abelmoschus moschatus Medik.", null));
4792    assertEquals("Abelmoschus moschatus tuberosus",
4793        parser.parseToCanonical("Abelmoschus moschatus subsp. tuberosus (Span.) Borss.Waalk.", null));
4794    assertEquals("Abia fasciata", parser.parseToCanonical("Abia fasciata (Linnaeus, 1758) (Linnaeus, 1758)", null));
4795    assertEquals("Abia fasciata", parser.parseToCanonical("Abia fasciata Linnaeus, 1758 Linnaeus, 1758", null));
4796    assertEquals("Abida secale", parser.parseToCanonical("Abida secale (Draparnaud, 1801) (Draparnaud) , 1801", null));
4797    assertEquals("Abida secale brauniopsis", parser.parseToCanonical("Abida secale brauniopsis Bofill i Poch, Artur", null));
4798    assertEquals("Abida secale inis", parser.parseToCanonical("Abida secale inis Bofill i Poch, Artur", null));
4799    assertEquals("Abida secale meridionalis",
4800        parser.parseToCanonical("Abida secale meridionalis Martínez Ortí, AlbertoGómez, BenjamínFaci, Guill", null));
4801    assertEquals("Abies alba", parser.parseToCanonical("Abies alba Abies alba Mill.", null));
4802    assertEquals("Abies alba", parser.parseToCanonical("Abies alba Abies alba Miller", null));
4803    assertEquals("Abies alba", parser.parseToCanonical("Abies alba Mill. (species) : Mill.", null));
4804    assertEquals("Abies amabilis",
4805        parser.parseToCanonical("Abies amabilis Abies amabilis (Dougl. ex Loud.) Dougl. ex Forbes", null));
4806    assertEquals("Abies amabilis", parser.parseToCanonical("Abies amabilis Abies amabilis Douglas ex Forbes", null));
4807    assertEquals("Abies arizonica", parser.parseToCanonical("Abies arizonica Abies arizonica Merriam", null));
4808    assertEquals("Abies balsamea", parser.parseToCanonical("Abies balsamea (L.) Mill. (species) : (L.) Mill.", null));
4809    assertEquals("Abies balsamea", parser.parseToCanonical("Abies balsamea (L.) Mill. / Ledeb.", null));
4810    assertEquals("Abies balsamea", parser.parseToCanonical("Abies balsamea Abies balsamea (L.) Mill.", null));
4811    assertEquals("Abelia grandiflora", parser.parseToCanonical("Abelia grandiflora Rehd (species) : Rehd", null));
4812  }

5235  @Test
5236  public void testNameParserIssue() throws Exception {
5237    // issue42
5238    ParsedName pn = parser.parse("Abacetus laevicollis de Chaudoir, 1869", null);
5239    assertEquals("Abacetus laevicollis", pn.canonicalNameWithMarker());
5240    assertEquals("de Chaudoir", pn.getAuthorship());
5241    assertEquals("1869", pn.getYear());
5242    assertTrue(1869 == pn.getYearInt());
5243    // issue50
5244    pn = parser.parse("Deinococcus-Thermus", null);
5245    assertEquals("Deinococcus-Thermus", pn.canonicalNameWithMarker());
5246    assertNull(pn.getAuthorship());
5247    assertNull(pn.getYear());
5248    // issue51
5249    pn = parser.parse("Alectis alexandrinus (Geoffroy St. Hilaire, 1817)", null);
5250    assertEquals("Alectis alexandrinus", pn.canonicalNameWithMarker());
5251    assertEquals("Geoffroy St. Hilaire", pn.getBracketAuthorship());
5252    assertEquals("1817", pn.getBracketYear());
5253    assertTrue(1817 == pn.getBracketYearInt());
5254    // issue60
5255    pn = parser.parse("Euphorbiaceae de Jussieu, 1789", null);
5256    assertEquals("Euphorbiaceae", pn.canonicalName());
5257    assertEquals("Euphorbiaceae", pn.getGenusOrAbove());
5258    assertEquals("de Jussieu", pn.getAuthorship());
5259    assertEquals("1789", pn.getYear());
5260  }

5342    assertEquals(Rank.SUBSPECIES, parser.parse("Coccyzuz ssp", null).getRank());

5344

5372  private ParsedName assertParsedInfrageneric(String name, Rank inputRank, String genus, String infrageneric, Rank rankMarker, String basAuthor, String basYear) throws UnparsableException {
5373    return assertParsedParts(name, inputRank, null, genus, infrageneric, null, null, rankMarker, null, null, null, basAuthor, basYear, null, null);
5374  }
5375
5376  private ParsedName assertParsedInfrageneric(String name, Rank inputRank, String genus, String infrageneric, Rank rankMarker, String author, String year, String basAuthor, String basYear) throws UnparsableException {
5377    return assertParsedParts(name, inputRank, null, genus, infrageneric, null, null, rankMarker, null, author, year, basAuthor, basYear, null, null);
5378  }
5379
5380  private ParsedName assertParsedParts(String name, String genus, String infrageneric, String epithet, String infraepithet,
5381                                       Rank rank, NamePart notho, String author, String year, String basAuthor, String basYear, String nomStatus) throws UnparsableException {
5382    return assertParsedParts(name, null, null, genus, infrageneric, epithet, infraepithet, rank, notho, author, year, basAuthor, basYear, nomStatus, null);
5383  }
5384
5385  private ParsedName assertParsedParts(String name, Rank inputRank, NameType type, String genus, String infrageneric, String epithet, String infraepithet,
5386                                       Rank rank, NamePart notho, String author, String year, String basAuthor, String basYear, String nomStatus, String strain)
5387      throws UnparsableException {
5388    ParsedName pn = parser.parse(name, inputRank);
5389    if (type != null) {
5390      assertEquals(type, pn.getType());
5391    }
5392    assertEquals(genus, pn.getGenusOrAbove());
5393    assertEquals(infrageneric, pn.getInfraGeneric());
5394    assertEquals(epithet, pn.getSpecificEpithet());
5395    assertEquals(infraepithet, pn.getInfraSpecificEpithet());
5396    if (rank != null) {
5397      assertEquals(rank, pn.getRank());
5398    }
5399    assertEquals(notho, pn.getNotho());
5400    assertEquals(author, pn.getAuthorship());
5401    assertEquals(year, pn.getYear());
5402    assertEquals(basAuthor, pn.getBracketAuthorship());
5403    assertEquals(basYear, pn.getBracketYear());
5404    assertEquals(nomStatus, pn.getNomStatus());
5405    assertEquals(strain, pn.getStrain());
5406
5407    return pn;
5408  }
5409
5410  private ParsedName assertParsedMicrobial(String name, NameType type, String genus, String epithet, String infraepithet,
5411                                           Rank rank, String strain) throws UnparsableException {
5412    return assertParsedMicrobial(name, type, genus, epithet, infraepithet, rank, null, null, null, null, strain);
5413  }
5414
5415  private ParsedName assertParsedMicrobial(String name, NameType type, String genus, String epithet, String infraepithet,
5416                                           Rank rank) throws UnparsableException {
5417    return assertParsedMicrobial(name, type, genus, epithet, infraepithet, rank, null, null, null, null, null);
5418  }
5419
5420  private ParsedName assertParsedMicrobial(String name, NameType type, String genus, String epithet, String infraepithet,
5421                                           Rank rank, String author, String year, String basAuthor, String basYear, String strain)
5422      throws UnparsableException {
5423    ParsedName pn = parser.parse(name, null);
5424    assertEquals(genus, pn.getGenusOrAbove());
5425    assertEquals(epithet, pn.getSpecificEpithet());
5426    assertEquals(infraepithet, pn.getInfraSpecificEpithet());
5427    assertEquals(rank, pn.getRank());
5428    assertEquals(author, pn.getAuthorship());
5429    assertEquals(year, pn.getYear());
5430    assertEquals(basAuthor, pn.getBracketAuthorship());
5431    assertEquals(basYear, pn.getBracketYear());
5432    assertEquals(strain, pn.getStrain());
5433    if (type != null) {
5434      assertEquals(type, pn.getType());
5435    }
5436    assertNull(pn.getNomStatus());
5437    assertNull(pn.getNotho());
5438    return pn;
5439  }
5440
5441  private ParsedName assertParsedName(String name, NameType type, String genus, String epithet, String infraepithet, Rank rank) {
5442    ParsedName pn = null;
5443    try {
5444      pn = assertParsedParts(name, null, type, genus, null, epithet, infraepithet, rank, null, null, null, null, null, null, null);
5445      assertEquals("Wrong name type", type, pn.getType());
5446    } catch (UnparsableException e) {
5447      assertEquals("Wrong name type", type, e.type);
5448    }
5449    return pn;
5450  }

5630  @Test
5631  public void testNameType() throws Exception {
5632    assertUnparsableType(NameType.HYBRID, "Asplenium rhizophyllum DC. x ruta-muraria E.L. Braun 1939");
5633    assertUnparsableType(NameType.HYBRID, "Agrostis L. × Polypogon Desf. ");
5634
5635    assertUnparsableType(NameType.VIRUS, "Cactus virus 2");
5636
5637    assertEquals(NameType.SCIENTIFIC, parser.parse("Neobisium carcinoides subsp. balcanicum Hadži, 1937", null).getType());
5638    assertEquals(NameType.SCIENTIFIC, parser.parse("Festulolium nilssonii Cugnac & A. Camus", null).getType());
5639    assertEquals(NameType.SCIENTIFIC, parser.parse("Coccyzuz americanus", null).getType());
5640    assertEquals(NameType.SCIENTIFIC, parser.parse("Tavila indeterminata Walker, 1869", null).getType());
5641    assertEquals(NameType.SCIENTIFIC, parser.parse("Phyllodonta indeterminata Schaus, 1901", null).getType());
5642    assertEquals(NameType.SCIENTIFIC, parser.parse("×Festulolium nilssonii Cugnac & A. Camus", null).getType());
5643
5644    // not using the multiplication sign, but an simple x
5645    assertEquals(NameType.SCIENTIFIC, parser.parse("x Festulolium nilssonii Cugnac & A. Camus", null).getType());
5646    assertEquals(NameType.SCIENTIFIC, parser.parse("xFestulolium nilssonii Cugnac & A. Camus", null).getType());
5647    assertEquals(NameType.SCIENTIFIC, parser.parse("nuculoidea behrens subsp. behrens var.christoph", null).getType());
5648    assertEquals(NameType.SCIENTIFIC, parser.parse("Neobisium (Neobisium) carcinoides balcanicum Hadži 1937", null).getType());
5649    assertEquals(NameType.SCIENTIFIC, parser.parse("Neobisium carcinoides ssp. balcanicum Hadži, 1937", null).getType());
5650    assertEquals(NameType.SCIENTIFIC,
5651        parser.parse("Valsa hypodermia sensu Berkeley & Broome (Not. Brit. Fungi no., 862)", null).getType());
5652    assertEquals(NameType.SCIENTIFIC, parser.parse("Solanum aculeatissimum auct. not Jacq.", null).getType());
5653
5654    assertEquals(NameType.INFORMAL, parser.parse("Coccyzuz cf americanus", null).getType());
5655    assertEquals(NameType.INFORMAL, parser.parse("Coccyzuz americanus ssp.", null).getType());
5656    assertEquals(NameType.INFORMAL, parser.parse("Asteraceae spec", null).getType());
5657
5658    assertEquals(NameType.DOUBTFUL, parser.parse("Callitrichia pilosa (Jocqu¿ & Scharff, 1986)", null).getType());
5659    assertEquals(NameType.DOUBTFUL, parser.parse("Sinopoda exspectata J¿ger & Ono, 2001", null).getType());
5660    assertEquals(NameType.DOUBTFUL, parser.parse("Callitrichia pilosa 1986 ?", null).getType());
5661    assertEquals(NameType.DOUBTFUL,
5662        parser.parse("Scaphytopius acutus delongi Young, 1952c:, 248 [n.sp. , not nom. nov.]", null).getType());
5663
5664  }

5740  /**
5741   * http://dev.gbif.org/issues/browse/POR-2508
5742   */
5743  @Test
5744  public void testNovNames() throws Exception {
5745
5746    ParsedName pn = parser.parse("Euphorbia rossiana var. nov. Steinmann, 1899", null);
5747    assertEquals("Euphorbia", pn.getGenusOrAbove());
5748    assertEquals("rossiana", pn.getSpecificEpithet());
5749    assertNull(pn.getInfraSpecificEpithet());
5750    assertEquals("Steinmann", pn.getAuthorship());
5751    assertEquals("1899", pn.getYear());
5752    assertEquals("var. nov.", pn.getNomStatus());
5753    assertEquals(Rank.VARIETY, pn.getRank());
5754
5755    pn = parser.parse("Ipomopsis tridactyla (Rydb.) Wilken, comb. nov. ined.", null);
5756    assertEquals("Ipomopsis", pn.getGenusOrAbove());
5757    assertEquals("tridactyla", pn.getSpecificEpithet());
5758    assertNull(pn.getInfraSpecificEpithet());
5759    assertEquals("Rydb.", pn.getBracketAuthorship());
5760    assertEquals("Wilken", pn.getAuthorship());
5761    assertNull(pn.getYear());
5762    assertEquals("comb. nov. ined.", pn.getNomStatus());
5763
5764    pn = parser.parse("Orobanche riparia Collins, sp. nov. ined.", null);

5829  @Test
5830  public void testNormalizeName() {
5831    assertEquals("Nuculoidea Williams et Breger, 1916", NameParser.normalize("Nuculoidea Williams et  Breger 1916  "));
5832    assertEquals("Nuculoidea behrens var. christoph Williams & Breger [1916]",
5833        NameParser.normalize("Nuculoidea behrens var.christoph Williams & Breger [1916]  "));
5834    assertEquals("Nuculoidea behrens var. christoph Williams & Breger [1916]",
5835        NameParser.normalize("Nuculoidea behrens var.christoph Williams & Breger [1916]  "));
5836    assertEquals(NameParser.normalize("Nuculoidea Williams & Breger, 1916  "),
5837        NameParser.normalize("Nuculoidea   Williams& Breger, 1916"));
5838    assertEquals("Asplenium ×inexpectatum (E.L. Braun, 1940) Morton (1956)",
5839        NameParser.normalize("Asplenium X inexpectatum (E.L. Braun 1940)Morton (1956) "));
5840    assertEquals("×Agropogon", NameParser.normalize(" × Agropogon"));
5841    assertEquals("Salix ×capreola Andersson", NameParser.normalize("Salix × capreola Andersson"));
5842    assertEquals("Leucanitis roda Herrich-Schäffer (1851), 1845",
5843        NameParser.normalize("Leucanitis roda Herrich-Schäffer (1851) 1845"));
5844
5845    assertEquals("Huaiyuanella Xing, Yan & Yin, 1984", NameParser.normalize("Huaiyuanella Xing, Yan&Yin, 1984"));
5846
5847  }
5848
5849  @Test
5850  public void testScientificNameStaysVerbatim() {
5851    for (String name : Lists.newArrayList(
5852        "Huaiyuanella Xing, Yan&Yin, 1984",
5853        "Abies alba agg.",
5854        "Trechus (Trechus) mogul Belousov & Kabak, 2001",
5855        "Trechus (Trechus) merditanus Apfelbeck, 1906"
5856    )) {
5857      assertEquals(name, parser.parseQuietly(name, null).getScientificName());
5858      assertEquals(name, parser.parseQuietly(name, Rank.SPECIES).getScientificName());
5859      assertEquals(name, parser.parseQuietly(name, Rank.INFRASPECIFIC_NAME).getScientificName());
5860    }
5861  }
5862
5863  @Test
5864  public void testNormalizeStrongName() {
5865    assertEquals("Nuculoidea Williams & Breger, 1916",
5866        NameParser.normalizeStrong("Nuculoidea Williams et  Breger 1916  "));
5867    assertEquals("Nuculoidea behrens var. christoph Williams & Breger, 1916",
5868        NameParser.normalizeStrong("Nuculoidea behrens var.christoph Williams & Breger [1916]  "));
5869    assertEquals("Nuculoidea Williams & Breger, 1916",
5870        NameParser.normalizeStrong(" 'Nuculoidea Williams & Breger, 1916'"));
5871    assertEquals("Malacocarpus schumannianus (Nicolai, 1893) Britton & Rose",
5872        NameParser.normalizeStrong("Malacocarpus schumannianus (Nicolai (1893)) Britton & Rose"));
5873    assertEquals("Photina (Cardioptera) burmeisteri (Westwood, 1889)",
5874        NameParser.normalizeStrong("Photina Cardioptera burmeisteri (Westwood 1889)"));
5875    assertEquals("Suaeda forsskahlei Schweinf.",
5876        NameParser.normalizeStrong("Suaeda forsskahlei Schweinf. ms."));
5877    assertEquals("Acacia bicolor Bojer", NameParser.normalizeStrong("Acacia bicolor Bojer ms."));
5878    assertEquals("Leucanitis roda (Herrich-Schäffer, 1851), 1845",
5879        NameParser.normalizeStrong("Leucanitis roda Herrich-Schäffer (1851) 1845"));
5880    assertEquals("Astelia alpina var. novae-hollandiae",
5881        NameParser.normalizeStrong("Astelia alpina var. novae-hollandiae"));
5882    // ampersand entities are handled as part of the regular html entity escaping:
5883    assertEquals("N. behrens Williams & amp; Breger, 1916",
5884        NameParser.normalizeStrong("  N.behrens Williams &amp;  Breger , 1916  "));
5885    assertEquals("N.behrens Williams & Breger , 1916",
5886        NameParser.preClean("  N.behrens Williams &amp;  Breger , 1916  "));
5887    assertEquals("N. behrens Williams & Breger, 1916",
5888        NameParser.normalizeStrong(NameParser.preClean("  N.behrens Williams &amp;  Breger , 1916  ")));
5889  }
5890
5891  @Test
5892  public void testOccNameFile() throws Exception {
5893    Reader reader = FileUtils.getInputStreamReader(streamUtils.classpathStream("parseNull.txt"));
5894    LineIterator iter = new LineIterator(reader);
5895
5896    int parseFails = 0;
5897    int parseAuthorless = 0;
5898    int lineNum = 0;
5899    long start = System.currentTimeMillis();
5900
5901    while (iter.hasNext()) {
5902      lineNum++;
5903      String name = iter.nextLine();
5904      ParsedName n;
5905      try {
5906        n = parser.parse(name, null);
5907        if (!n.isAuthorsParsed()) {
5908          parseAuthorless++;
5909          LOG.warn("NO AUTHORS\t " + name);
5910        }
5911      } catch (UnparsableException e) {
5912        parseFails++;
5913        LOG.warn("FAIL\t " + name);
5914      }
5915    }
5916    long end = System.currentTimeMillis();
5917    LOG.info("\n\nNames tested: " + lineNum);
5918    LOG.info("Names parse fail: " + parseFails);
5919    LOG.info("Names parse no authors: " + parseAuthorless);
5920    LOG.info("Total time: " + (end - start));
5921    LOG.info("Average per name: " + (((double) end - start) / lineNum));
5922
5923    int currFail = 2;
5924    if ((parseFails) > currFail) {
5925      fail("We are getting worse, not better. Currently failing: " + (parseFails) + ". Was passing:" + currFail);
5926    }
5927    int currNoAuthors = 109;
5928    if ((parseAuthorless) > currNoAuthors) {
5929      fail(
5930          "We are getting worse, not better. Currently without authors: " + (parseAuthorless) + ". Was:" + currNoAuthors);
5931    }
5932  }

5942      // nothing, expected to fail
5943    }
5944    try {
5945      n = parser.parse("(1-SFS)%20Aster%20lowrieanus%20Porter", null);
5946      parsed = true;
5947    } catch (UnparsableException e) {
5948      // nothing, expected to fail
5949    }
5950  }

6129   * http://dev.gbif.org/issues/browse/POR-2988
6130   */
6131  @Test
6132  public void testDoubleEtAl() throws Exception {
6133    ParsedName pn = parser.parse("Hymenopus coronatoides Wang & et al., 1994", null);
6134    assertEquals("Hymenopus", pn.getGenusOrAbove());
6135    assertEquals("coronatoides", pn.getSpecificEpithet());
6136    assertEquals("Wang et al.", pn.getAuthorship());
6137    assertEquals("1994", pn.getYear());
6138    assertEquals(NameType.SCIENTIFIC, pn.getType());
6139
6140    pn = parser.parse("Hymenopus coronatoides Wang & & et & al., 1994", null);
6141    assertEquals("Hymenopus", pn.getGenusOrAbove());
6142    assertEquals("coronatoides", pn.getSpecificEpithet());
6143    assertEquals("Wang et al.", pn.getAuthorship());
6144    assertEquals("1994", pn.getYear());
6145    assertEquals(NameType.SCIENTIFIC, pn.getType());
6146  }

6151    assertTrue(isViralName("Cactus virus 2"));
6152    assertTrue(isViralName("Suid herpesvirus 3 Ictv"));
6153    assertTrue(isViralName("Tomato yellow leaf curl Mali virus Ictv"));
6154    assertTrue(isViralName("Not Sapovirus MC10"));
6155    assertTrue(isViralName("Diolcogaster facetosa bracovirus"));
6156    assertTrue(isViralName("Human papillomavirus"));
6157    assertTrue(isViralName("Sapovirus Hu/GI/Nsc, 150/PA/Bra/, 1993"));
6158    assertTrue(isViralName("Aspergillus mycovirus, 1816"));
6159    assertTrue(isViralName("Hantavirus sdp2 Yxl-, 2008"));
6160    assertTrue(isViralName("Norovirus Nizhny Novgorod /, 2461 / Rus /, 2007"));

6183  @Test
6184  public void testBacteriaNames() throws Exception {
6185    assertUnparsableDoubtful("HMWdDNA-degrading marine bacterium 10");
6186    assertUnparsableDoubtful("SAR11 cluster bacterium enrichment culture clone Pshtc-, 019");
6187    assertUnparsableDoubtful("SR1 bacterium canine oral taxon, 369");
6188    assertUnparsableDoubtful("bacterium 'glyphosate'");
6189    assertUnparsableDoubtful("bacterium 'hafez'");
6190    assertUnparsableDoubtful("bacterium A1");
6191  }
6192
6193  public boolean isViralName(String name) {
6194    try {
6195      ParsedName pn = parser.parse(name, null);
6196    } catch (UnparsableException e) {
6197      // swallow
6198      if (NameType.VIRUS == e.type) {
6199        return true;
6200      }
6201    }
6202    return false;
6203  }

6209    assertNull(n.getInfraGeneric());
6210    assertEquals("attenuata", n.getSpecificEpithet());
6211    assertNull(n.getInfraSpecificEpithet());
6212    assertEquals("Hincks", n.getAuthorship());
6213    assertEquals("1866", n.getYear());
6214    assertEquals(NameType.PLACEHOLDER, n.getType());
6215  }

6239    assertNull(n.getInfraGeneric());
6240    assertNull(n.getSpecificEpithet());

6243    assertNull(n.getYear());
6244    assertEquals(NameType.INFORMAL, n.getType());
6245    assertEquals(Rank.SPECIES, n.getRank());
6246    assertEquals("Elmis spec.", n.canonicalNameComplete());
6247
6248    n = parser.parse("Elmis sp. Lv", Rank.SPECIES);
6249    assertEquals("Elmis", n.getGenusOrAbove());
6250    assertNull(n.getInfraGeneric());
6251    assertNull(n.getSpecificEpithet());
6252    assertNull(n.getInfraSpecificEpithet());
6253    assertNull(n.getAuthorship());
6254    assertNull(n.getYear());
6255    assertEquals(NameType.INFORMAL, n.getType());
6256    assertEquals(Rank.SPECIES, n.getRank());
6257    assertEquals("Elmis spec.", n.canonicalNameComplete());
6258
6259    n = parser.parse("Elmis sp. Ad.", null);
6260    assertEquals("Elmis", n.getGenusOrAbove());
6261    assertNull(n.getInfraGeneric());
6262    assertNull(n.getSpecificEpithet());
6263    assertNull(n.getInfraSpecificEpithet());
6264    assertNull(n.getAuthorship());
6265    assertNull(n.getYear());
6266    assertEquals(NameType.INFORMAL, n.getType());
6267    assertEquals(Rank.SPECIES, n.getRank());
6268    assertEquals("Elmis spec.", n.canonicalNameComplete());
6269

6271    assertEquals("Elmis", n.getGenusOrAbove());
6272    assertNull(n.getInfraGeneric());
6273    assertNull(n.getSpecificEpithet());

6278    assertEquals(Rank.SUBSPECIES, n.getRank());
6279    assertEquals("Elmis subsp.", n.canonicalNameComplete());

6285  @Test
6286  public void parseProblematicSpecies() throws Exception {
6287    ParsedName n = parser.parse("Angiopteris d'urvilleana de Vriese", Rank.SPECIES);
6288    assertEquals("Angiopteris", n.getGenusOrAbove());
6289    assertNull(n.getInfraGeneric());
6290    assertEquals("d'urvilleana", n.getSpecificEpithet());
6291    assertNull(n.getInfraSpecificEpithet());
6292    assertEquals("de Vriese", n.getAuthorship());
6293    assertEquals(NameType.SCIENTIFIC, n.getType());
6294
6295    n = parser.parse("Polana (Bulbusana) vana DeLong & Freytag 1972", Rank.SPECIES);
6296    assertEquals("Polana", n.getGenusOrAbove());
6297    assertEquals("Bulbusana", n.getInfraGeneric());
6298    assertEquals("vana", n.getSpecificEpithet());
6299    assertNull(n.getInfraSpecificEpithet());
6300    assertEquals("DeLong & Freytag", n.getAuthorship());
6301    assertEquals("1972", n.getYear());
6302    assertEquals(NameType.SCIENTIFIC, n.getType());
6303
6304    n = parser.parse("Tabanus 4punctatus Fabricius, 1805", Rank.SPECIES);
6305    assertEquals("Tabanus", n.getGenusOrAbove());
6306    assertNull(n.getInfraGeneric());
6307    assertEquals("4punctatus", n.getSpecificEpithet());
6308    assertNull(n.getInfraSpecificEpithet());
6309    assertEquals("Fabricius", n.getAuthorship());
6310    assertEquals("1805", n.getYear());
6311    assertEquals(NameType.SCIENTIFIC, n.getType());
6312
6313    n = parser.parse("Acer √ó hillieri Lancaster", Rank.SPECIES);
6314    assertEquals("Acer", n.getGenusOrAbove());
6315    assertNull(n.getInfraGeneric());
6316    assertEquals("hillieri", n.getSpecificEpithet());
6317    assertEquals(NamePart.SPECIFIC, n.getNotho());
6318    assertEquals("Acer ×hillieri Lancaster", n.canonicalNameComplete());
6319    assertEquals("Acer ×hillieri Lancaster", n.fullName());
6320    //assertEquals("Acer × hillieri Lancaster", n.getScientificName());
6321    assertNull(n.getInfraSpecificEpithet());
6322    assertEquals("Lancaster", n.getAuthorship());
6323    assertNull(n.getYear());
6324    // the garbage hybrid cross makes this doubtful
6325    assertEquals(NameType.DOUBTFUL, n.getType());
6326
6327  }

6330  @Test
6331  public void testWhitespaceEpitheta() throws Exception {
6332    ParsedName n = parser.parse("Nupserha van rooni usambarica", null);
6333    assertEquals("Nupserha", n.getGenusOrAbove());
6334    assertNull(n.getInfraGeneric());
6335    assertEquals("van rooni", n.getSpecificEpithet());
6336    assertEquals("usambarica", n.getInfraSpecificEpithet());
6337
6338    n = parser.parse("Sargassum flavicans van pervillei", null);
6339    assertEquals("Sargassum", n.getGenusOrAbove());
6340    assertNull(n.getInfraGeneric());
6341    assertEquals("flavicans", n.getSpecificEpithet());
6342    assertEquals("van pervillei", n.getInfraSpecificEpithet());
6343
6344    n = parser.parse("Salix novae angliae lingulata ", null);
6345    assertEquals("Salix", n.getGenusOrAbove());
6346    assertNull(n.getInfraGeneric());
6347    assertEquals("novae angliae", n.getSpecificEpithet());
6348    assertEquals("lingulata", n.getInfraSpecificEpithet());
6349
6350    n = parser.parse("Ilex collina van trompii", null);
6351    assertEquals("Ilex", n.getGenusOrAbove());
6352    assertNull(n.getInfraGeneric());
6353    assertEquals("collina", n.getSpecificEpithet());
6354    assertEquals("van trompii", n.getInfraSpecificEpithet());
6355
6356    n = parser.parse("Gaultheria depressa novae zealandiae", null);
6357    assertEquals("Gaultheria", n.getGenusOrAbove());
6358    assertNull(n.getInfraGeneric());
6359    assertEquals("depressa", n.getSpecificEpithet());
6360    assertEquals("novae zealandiae", n.getInfraSpecificEpithet());
6361
6362    n = parser.parse("Caraguata van volxemi gracilior", null);
6363    assertEquals("Caraguata", n.getGenusOrAbove());
6364    assertNull(n.getInfraGeneric());
6365    assertEquals("van volxemi", n.getSpecificEpithet());
6366    assertEquals("gracilior", n.getInfraSpecificEpithet());
6367

6369    assertEquals("Ancistrocerus", n.getGenusOrAbove());
6370    assertNull(n.getInfraGeneric());
6371    assertEquals("agilis", n.getSpecificEpithet());
6372    assertEquals("novae guineae", n.getInfraSpecificEpithet());
6373
6374    // also test the authorless parsing
6375    n = parser.parse("Ancistrocerus agilis novae guineae", null);
6376    assertEquals("Ancistrocerus", n.getGenusOrAbove());
6377    assertNull(n.getInfraGeneric());
6378    assertEquals("agilis", n.getSpecificEpithet());
6379    assertEquals("novae guineae", n.getInfraSpecificEpithet());
